///--- BEGINNING OF MODULE ---

'====================================================================================================
' Macro modificada 2012-Jun-15 por +
'====================================================================================================
Sub Genera_bd_con_CAT()

Application.ScreenUpdating = False
Application.StatusBar = "Iniciando cálculo..."

Dim SourceData As Range
Set SourceData = [BD_ORIGEN_INICIO].CurrentRegion

For ciclo = 2 To SourceData.Rows.Count
    
    If SourceData.Rows(ciclo).Cells(18).Formula = "" Then
        SourceData.Rows(ciclo).Copy
    
        Sheets("Tabla_CAT").Rows(2).PasteSpecial Paste:=xlValues
      
        [RESULTADO_CALCULOS].Copy
        
        SourceData.Rows(ciclo).Cells(18).PasteSpecial Paste:=xlValues
    Else
        Debug.Print "Fila " & ciclo & " ya procesada..."
    End If
        
    DoEvents
    If ciclo Mod 10 = 0 Then Application.StatusBar = "Fila " & ciclo
Next ciclo

Application.ScreenUpdating = True
SourceData.Columns(1).Cells(SourceData.Rows.Count).Select

Application.CutCopyMode = False
Application.StatusBar = False


End Sub

Sub BorrarAreaDeResultados()
    Set BD_DESTINO = [BD_DESTINO_INICIO].CurrentRegion
    If BD_DESTINO.Rows.Count > 1 Then
    Range( _
        [BD_DESTINO_INICIO].Rows(2), _
        BD_DESTINO.Cells(BD_DESTINO.Cells.Count) _
        ).ClearContents
    End If

End Sub

[Timer] 54 líneas de código.
///--- BEGINNING OF MODULE ---
Private Declare Function getFrequency Lib "kernel32" _
Alias "QueryPerformanceFrequency" (cyFrequency As Currency) As Long
Private Declare Function getTickCount Lib "kernel32" _
Alias "QueryPerformanceCounter" (cyTickCount As Currency) As Long
' Nos regresa el número de segundos
Function MicroTimer() As Double

Dim cyTicks1 As Currency
Static cyFrequency As Currency
MicroTimer = 0

' Pedimos la frecuencia
If cyFrequency = 0 Then getFrequency cyFrequency

' Luego los ticks
getTickCount cyTicks1

' Y calculamos los segundos.
If cyFrequency Then MicroTimer = cyTicks1 / cyFrequency
End Function

Sub Cronometra()
Dim dTime As Double
Dim dAcumTime As Double
Dim NumPruebas As Integer
NumPruebas = 1

Dim Mensaje As String

For i = 1 To NumPruebas
    
    'BorrarAreaDeResultados
    
    dTime = MicroTimer()
    
    Genera_bd_con_CAT
    
    dTime = MicroTimer - dTime
    dAcumTime = dAcumTime + dTime
    dTime = Round(dTime, 2)
    
    EsteMensaje = "- Corrida " & CStr(i) & " terminada en " & CStr(dTime) & " segundos."
    Mensaje = Mensaje & vbCrLf & EsteMensaje
    Debug.Print EsteMensaje

Next

EsteMensaje = ""
If NumPruebas > 1 Then EsteMensaje = "Promedio " & Round(dAcumTime / NumPruebas, 2) & " segundos."
Mensaje = "Proceso terminado." & vbCrLf & Mensaje & vbCrLf & EsteMensaje
Debug.Print EsteMensaje

MsgBox Mensaje
End Sub
\\\--- END OF MODULE ---
